#
# Unicode mapping for JIS C 6226:1978 (retronymously JIS X 0208:1978) with NEC PC98 extensions.
# Amended 2019-02 with additional deviations from modern mappings to fully use the closest matches
#   in the 1990-JIS (including JIS X 0212) repertoire (although U+663B/U+6602 were still their
#   Microsoft way around, as an oversight on my part).
# Further amended 2021-08-05 to swap U+663B/U+6602 and use some closer 2004-JIS and other characters:
#   20-34: now U+3D4E, was U+6F97
#   25-23: now U+663B, was U+6602 (compare 90-22)
#   26-84: now U+6805 (GB 2312), was U+67F5
#   32-70: now U+87EC (2000-JIS level 3), was U+8749
#   34-45: now U+9A52 (2000-JIS level 3), was U+9A28
#   35-29: now U+7C1E (2000-JIS level 3), was U+7BAA
#   39-77: now U+525D (2004-JIS level 3), was U+5265
#   53-67: now U+21A1A, was U+5BC3
#   54-02: now U+5C5B (2004-JIS level 3), was U+5C4F
#   90-22: now U+6602, was U+663B (compare 25-23)
# Further amended 2021-08-12 referencing NEC-specific CIDs, double-checked against bitmap font:
#   17-28: kept as U+958F; changing to U+28CDD per CID map is not justified by bitmap font
#   23-46: now U+25874, was U+7A3D
#   23-53: now U+8346, was U+834A
#   23-68: now U+28EF6, was U+9699
#   59-42: now U+67FA, was U+67B4
#   59-84: now U+688E, was U+688D
#   63-83: kept as U+71D7; changing to U+243D0 per CID map is not justified by bitmap font
#   73-28: kept as U+85DC; changing to U+853E per CID map is not justified by bitmap font
#   80-19: kept as U+96CE; changing to U+7762 per CID map is not justified by bitmap font
#
# NEC's double byte character set makes substantial use of halfwidth-fullwidth distinctions which
# cannot be represented in Unicode. Following a convention established by Apple, W (naturally wide)
# or A (ambiguous width) codepoints followed by the private use codepoint f87f indicate halfwidth.
#
